## MODEL âœ¨

ç¾åœ¨ï¼Œæˆ‘è¦å°‡ `js/script.js` çš„å…§å®¹æ›¿æ›ç‚ºå®Œæ•´çš„æ¸¬é©—é‚è¼¯ã€‚**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "const startButton = document.getElementById('start-btn');\nconst quizContainer = document.getElementById('quiz-container');\nconst questionElement = document.getElementById('question');\nconst answerButtonsElement = document.getElementById('answer-buttons');\nconst nextButton = document.getElementById('next-btn');\nconst timerElement = document.getElementById('timer');\n\nlet shuffledQuestions, currentQuestionIndex;\nlet score = 0;\nlet timer;\nlet timeRemaining = 30;\n\nstartButton.addEventListener('click', startQuiz);\nnextButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n    currentQuestionIndex++;\n    setNextQuestion();\n});\n\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    startButton.style.display = 'none';\n startTimer();\n}\n\nfunction setNextQuestion() {\n    resetState();\n    if (currentQuestionIndex < shuffledQuestions.length) {\n        showQuestion(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    clearStatusClass(document.body);\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct;\n    setStatusClass(document.body, correct);\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct);\n    });\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n }\n}\n\nfunction clearStatusClass(element) {\n    element.classList.remove('correct');\n    element.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n ## MODEL âœ¨

æˆ‘ç¾åœ¨è¦ä¾†ä¿®æ­£ `js/script.js` çš„å•é¡Œã€‚

ä¿®æ”¹å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

1.  **`selectAnswer` å‡½å¼ï¼š**
    *   ä¸å†è¨­å®š `document.body` çš„ç‹€æ…‹ classã€‚

```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "const startButton = document.getElementById('start-btn');\nconst quizContainer = document.getElementById('quiz-container');\nconst questionElement = document.getElementById('question');\nconst answerButtonsElement = document.getElementById('answer-buttons');\nconst nextButton = document.getElementById('next-btn');\nconst timerElement = document.getElementById('timer');\nconst searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');\nconst subjectFilter = document.getElementById('subject-filter');\nconst filterButton = document.getElementById('filter-btn');\n\nlet allQuestions = questions;\nlet filteredQuestions = allQuestions;\nlet shuffledQuestions, currentQuestionIndex;\nlet score = 0;\nlet timer;\nlet timeRemaining = 30;\n\n// Populate subjects and set up event listeners when the script loads\ndocument.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n    populateSubjects();\n    filterButton.addEventListener('click', filterQuestions);\n    startButton.addEventListener('click', startQuiz);\n    nextButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        currentQuestionIndex++;\n        setNextQuestion();\n    });\n});\n\nfunction populateSubjects() {\n    const subjects = [...new Set(allQuestions.map(q => q.subject))];\n    subjects.forEach(subject => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = subject;\n        option.innerText = subject;\n        subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    filteredQuestions = allQuestions.filter(question => {\n        const subjectMatch = selectedSubject === 'all' || question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        return subjectMatch && searchMatch;\n    });\n\n    // Automatically start the quiz with the filtered questions\n    startQuiz();\n}\n\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    startButton.style.display = 'none';\n    quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) {\n        endResult.remove();\n    }\n    \n    questionElement.style.display = 'block';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'grid';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'block';\n\n    shuffledQuestions = filteredQuestions.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n document.getElementById('question');\nconst answerButtonsElement = document.getElementById('answer-buttons');\nconst nextButton = document.getElementById('next-btn');\nconst timerElement = document.getElementById('timer');\nconst searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');\nconst subjectFilter = document.getElementById('subject-filter');\nconst filterButton = document.getElementById('filter-btn');\n\nlet allQuestions = questions;\nlet filteredQuestions = allQuestions;\nlet shuffledQuestions, currentQuestionIndex;\nlet score = 0;\nlet timer;\nlet timeRemaining = 30;\n\n// Populate subjects and set up event listeners when the script loads\ndocument.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n    populateSubjects();\n    filterButton.addEventListener('click', filterQuestions);\n    startButton.addEventListener('click', startQuiz);\n    nextButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        currentQuestionIndex++;\n        setNextQuestion();\n    });\n});\n\nfunction populateSubjects() {\n    const subjects = [...new Set(allQuestions.map(q => q.subject))];\n    subjects.forEach(subject => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = subject;\n        option.innerText = subject;\n        subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    filteredQuestions = allQuestions.filter(question => {\n        const subjectMatch = selectedSubject === 'all' || question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        return subjectMatch && searchMatch;\n    });\n\n    // Automatically start the quiz with the filtered questions\n    startQuiz();\n}\n\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    startButton.style.display = 'none';\n    quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) {\n        endResult.remove();\n    }\n    \n    questionElement.style.display = 'block';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'grid';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'block';\n\n    shuffledQuestions = filteredQuestions.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.innerText = 'æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„é¡Œç›®ï¼Œè«‹é‡æ–°ç¯©é¸ã€‚';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    startButton.style.display = 'block';\n    startButton.innerText = 'è¿”å›';\n}\n\n\nfunction setNextQuestion() {\n    resetState();\n    if (currentQuestionIndex < shuffledQuestions.length) {\n        showQuestion(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n        startTimer();\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous answers\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    }\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction setButtonStatusClass(button, correct) {\n    clearButtonStatusClass(button);\n    if (correct) {\n        button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n        timeRemaining--;\n        timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n        if (timeRemaining <= 0) {\n            clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction timeUp() {\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, false);\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n     clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\n\nfunction endQuiz() {\n    clearInterval(timer);\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.style.display = 'none';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'none';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    \n    const endResult = document.createElement('div');\n    endResult.classList.add('end-result');\n    endResult.innerHTML = `\n        <h2>æ¸¬é©—çµæŸï¼</h2>\n        <p>ä½ çš„åˆ†æ•¸æ˜¯ ${score} / ${shuffledQuestions.length}</p>\n        <button id=\"restart-btn\">é‡æ–°é–‹å§‹</button>\n    `;\n    quizContainer.appendChild(endResult);\n    \n    document.getElementById('restart-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n        // Instead of reloading, we just show the filter container again\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        startButton.style.display = 'block';\n        document.getElementById('filter-container').style.display = 'flex';\n    });\n}\n"
  }

{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "const quizContainer = document.getElementById('quiz-container');\nconst questionElement = document.getElementById('question');\nconst answerButtonsElement = timeRemaining = 30;\n\ndocument.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n    populateSubjects();\n    startQuizButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        filterQuestions();\n        startQuiz();\n    });\n    nextButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        currentQuestionIndex++;\n        setNextQuestion();\n    });\n});\n\nfunction populateSubjects() {\n    const subjects = [...new Set(allQuestions.map(q => q.subject))];\n    subjects.forEach(subject => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = subject;\n        option.innerText = subject;\n        subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    filteredQuestions = allQuestions.filter(question => {\n        const subjectMatch = selectedSubject === 'all' || question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        return subjectMatch && searchMatch;\n    });\n}\n\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) {\n        endResult.remove();\n    }\n    \n    questionElement.style.display = 'block';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'grid';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'block';\n\n    shuffledQuestions = filteredQuestions.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.innerText = 'æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„é¡Œç›®ï¼Œè«‹é‡æ–°ç¯©é¸ã€‚';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous answers\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    }\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n {
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "const quizContainer = document.getElementById('quiz-container');\nconst questionElement = document.getElementById('question');\nconst answerButtonsElement = {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous answers\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswers.push(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n    }\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction setButtonStatusClass(button, correct) {\n    clearButtonStatusClass(button);\n    if (correct) {\n        button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n        timeRemaining--;\n        timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n        if (timeRemaining <= 0) {\n            clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction timeUp() {\n    wrongAnswers.push(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, false);\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n     clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\n\nfunction endQuiz() {\n    clearInterval(timer);\n    saveProgress();\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.style.display = 'none';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'none';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    \n    const endResult = document.createElement('div');\n    endResult.classList.add('end-result');\n    endResult.innerHTML = `\n        <h2>æ¸¬é©—çµæŸï¼</h2>\n        <p>ä½ çš„åˆ†æ•¸æ˜¯ ${score} / ${shuffledQuestions.length}</p>\n        <button id=\"restart-btn\">è¿”å›ä¸»é </button>\n    `;\n    quizContainer.appendChild(endResult);\n    \n    document.getElementById('restart-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    });\n}\n\nfunction saveProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    const subject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    if (!progress[subject]) {\n        progress[subject] = { totalScore: 0, totalQuestions: 0, wrongAnswers: [] };\n    }\n\n    progress[subject].totalScore += score;\n    progress[subject].totalQuestions += shuffledQuestions.length;\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers.push(...wrongAnswers);\n\n    // Keep only unique wrong answers\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers = [...new Map(progress[subject].wrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n\n    localStorage.setItem('quizProgress', JSON.stringify(progress));\n}\n\nfunction toggleProgressView() {\n    if (progressContainer.style.display === 'none') {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';\n        showProgress();\n    } else {\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    progressStats.innerHTML = '';\n\n    let totalScore = 0;\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? progress[subject].totalQuestions += shuffledQuestions.length;\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers.push(...wrongAnswers);\n\n    // åˆ©ç”¨ Map å»é™¤é‡è¤‡çš„éŒ¯é¡Œ\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers = [...new Map(progress[subject].wrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    localStorage.setItem('quizProgress', JSON.stringify(progress));\n}\n\n/**\n * @description åˆ‡æ›å­¸ç¿’é€²åº¦è¦–åœ–\n */\nfunction toggleProgressView() {\n    if (progressContainer.style.display === 'none') {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';\n        showProgress();\n    } else {\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * @description é¡¯ç¤ºå­¸ç¿’é€²åº¦\n */\nfunction showProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    progressStats.innerHTML = '';\n\n    let totalScore = 0;\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    // è¨ˆç®—ä¸¦é¡¯ç¤ºå„ç§‘é€²åº¦\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? 'ç¸½è¦½' : subject}</h3>\n            <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n                <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${percentage}%\">${percentage}%</div>\n            </div>\n            <p>ç­”å° ${progress[subject].totalScore} / ${progress[subject].totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n        `;\n        progressStats.appendChild(subjectStat);\n    }\n\n    // è¨ˆç®—ä¸¦é¡¯ç¤ºç¸½é«”é€²åº¦\n    const overallPercentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (totalScore / totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n    const overallStat = document.createElement('div');\n    overallStat.innerHTML = `\n        <h3>ç¸½é«”é€²åº¦</h3>\n        <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n            <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${overallPercentage}%\">${overallPercentage}%</div>\n        </div>\n        <p>ç¸½ç­”å° ${totalScore} / ${totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n    `;\n    progressStats.prepend(overallStat);\n\n    // é¡¯ç¤ºæ‰€æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œ\n    const wrongAnswersContainer = document.createElement('div');\n    wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML = '<h3>éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„</h3>';\n    let allWrongAnswers = [];\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        allWrongAnswers.push(...progress[subject].wrongAnswers);\n    }\n    allWrongAnswers = [...new Map(allWrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    if (allWrongAnswers.length > 0) {\n        const list = document.createElement('ul');\n        allWrongAnswers.forEach(q => {\n            const item = document.createElement('li');\n            item.innerText = q.question;\n            list.appendChild(item);\n        });\n        wrongAnswersContainer.appendChild(list);\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML += '<p>æ²’æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„ï¼</p>';\n    }\n    progressStats.appendChild(wrongAnswersContainer);\n}\n"
  }
}

æ ¹æ“š allQuestions å‹•æ…‹ç”Ÿæˆç§‘ç›®ç¯©é¸çš„ä¸‹æ‹‰é¸å–®\n */\nfunction populateSubjects() {\n    const subjects = [...new Set(allQuestions.map(q => q.subject))]; // åˆ©ç”¨ Set å»é™¤é‡è¤‡çš„ç§‘ç›®\n subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * @description æ ¹æ“šæœå°‹é—œéµå­—å’Œé¸æ“‡çš„ç§‘ç›®ç¯©é¸é¡Œç›®\n */\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    filteredQuestions = allQuestions.filter(question => {\n        const subjectMatch = selectedSubject === 'all' || question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        return subjectMatch && searchMatch;\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * @description é–‹å§‹æ¸¬é©—\n */\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    // UI ç‹€æ…‹æ›´æ–°\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) {\n        endResult.remove();\n    }\n    \n    questionElement.style.display = 'block';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'grid';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'block';\n\n    // åˆå§‹åŒ–æ¸¬é©—ç‹€æ…‹\n    shuffledQuestions = filteredQuestions.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5); // éš¨æ©Ÿæ’åºé¡Œç›®\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n    wrongAnswers = [];\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * @description ç•¶æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„é¡Œç›®æ™‚é¡¯ç¤ºæç¤º\n */\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.innerText = 'æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„é¡Œç›®ï¼Œè«‹é‡æ–°ç¯©é¸ã€‚';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n}\n\n/**\n * @description è¨­å®šä¸‹ä¸€é¡Œ\n */\nfunction setNextQuestion() {\n    resetState();\n    if (currentQuestionIndex < shuffledQuestions.length) {\n        showQuestion(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n        startTimer();\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * @description é¡¯ç¤ºç•¶å‰é¡Œç›®åŠç­”æ¡ˆé¸é …\n * @param {object} question \n */\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = ''; // æ¸…ç©ºå…ˆå‰çš„ç­”æ¡ˆ\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * @description é‡ç½®é¡Œç›®ç‹€æ…‹ (æ¸…ç©ºç­”æ¡ˆã€éš±è—ä¸‹ä¸€é¡ŒæŒ‰éˆ•)\n */\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * @description é¸æ“‡ç­”æ¡ˆå¾Œçš„è™•ç†\n * @param {Event} e \n */\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n\n    // é¡¯ç¤ºæ‰€æœ‰ç­”æ¡ˆçš„å°éŒ¯ç‹€æ…‹ä¸¦ç¦ç”¨æŒ‰éˆ•\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswers.push(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n    }\n\n    // åˆ¤æ–·æ˜¯å¦é‚„æœ‰ä¸‹ä¸€é¡Œ\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\n/**\n * @description è¨­å®šæŒ‰éˆ•çš„å°éŒ¯æ¨£å¼\n * @param {HTMLElement} button \n * @param {boolean} correct \n */\nfunction setButtonStatusClass(button, correct) {\n    clearButtonStatusClass(button);\n    if (correct) {\n        button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * @description æ¸…é™¤æŒ‰éˆ•çš„å°éŒ¯æ¨£å¼\n * @param {HTMLElement} button \n */\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\n/**\n * @description é–‹å§‹è¨ˆæ™‚å™¨\n */\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n        timeRemaining--;\n        timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n        if (timeRemaining <= 0) {\n            clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\n/**\n * @description æ™‚é–“åˆ°ï¼Œè‡ªå‹•è·³åˆ°ä¸‹ä¸€é¡Œ\n */\nfunction timeUp() {\n    wrongAnswers.push(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, false);\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n     clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\n/**\n * @description çµæŸæ¸¬é©—\n */\nfunction endQuiz() {\n    clearInterval(timer);\n    saveProgress(); // å„²å­˜é€²åº¦\n    resetState();\n    // UI æ›´æ–°\n    questionElement.style.display = 'none';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'none';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    \n    // é¡¯ç¤ºçµæœ\n    const endResult = document.createElement('div');\n    endResult.classList.add('end-result');\n    endResult.innerHTML = `\n        <h2>æ¸¬é©—çµæŸï¼</h2>\n        <p>ä½ çš„åˆ†æ•¸æ˜¯ ${score} / ${shuffledQuestions.length}</p>\n        <button id=\"restart-btn\">è¿”å›ä¸»é </button>\n    `;\n    quizContainer.appendChild(endResult);\n    \n    // è¿”å›ä¸»é æŒ‰éˆ•äº‹ä»¶\n    document.getElementById('restart-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * @description å„²å­˜æ¸¬é©—é€²åº¦åˆ° Local Storage\n */\nfunction saveProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    const subject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    if (!progress[subject]) {\n        progress[subject] = { totalScore: 0, totalQuestions: 0, wrongAnswers: [] };\n    }\n\n    progress[subject].totalScore += score;\n    progress[subject].totalQuestions += shuffledQuestions.length;\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers.push(...wrongAnswers);\n\n    // åˆ©ç”¨ Map å»é™¤é‡è¤‡çš„éŒ¯é¡Œ\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers = [...new Map(progress[subject].wrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    localStorage.setItem('quizProgress', JSON.stringify(progress));\n}\n\n/**\n * @description åˆ‡æ›å­¸ç¿’é€²åº¦è¦–åœ–\n */\nfunction toggleProgressView() {\n    if (progressContainer.style.display === 'none') {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';\n        showProgress();\n    } else {\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * @description é¡¯ç¤ºå­¸ç¿’é€²åº¦\n */\nfunction showProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    progressStats.innerHTML = '';\n\n    let totalScore = 0;\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    // è¨ˆç®—ä¸¦é¡¯ç¤ºå„ç§‘é€²åº¦\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? 'ç¸½è¦½' : subject}</h3>\n            <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n                <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${percentage}%\">${percentage}%</div>\n            </div>\n            <p>ç­”å° ${progress[subject].totalScore} / ${progress[subject].totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n        `;\n        progressStats.appendChild(subjectStat);\n    }\n\n    // è¨ˆç®—ä¸¦é¡¯ç¤ºç¸½é«”é€²åº¦\n    const overallPercentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (totalScore / totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n    const overallStat = document.createElement('div');\n    overallStat.innerHTML = `\n        <h3>ç¸½é«”é€²åº¦</h3>\n        <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n            <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${overallPercentage}%\">${overallPercentage}%</div>\n        </div>\n        <p>ç¸½ç­”å° ${totalScore} / ${totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n    `;\n    progressStats.prepend(overallStat);\n\n    // é¡¯ç¤ºæ‰€æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œ\n    const wrongAnswersContainer = document.createElement('div');\n    wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML = '<h3>éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„</h3>';\n    let allWrongAnswers = [];\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        allWrongAnswers.push(...progress[subject].wrongAnswers);\n    }\n    allWrongAnswers = [...new Map(allWrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    if (allWrongAnswers.length > 0) {\n        const list = document.createElement('ul');\n        allWrongAnswers.forEach(q => {\n            const item = document.createElement('li');\n            item.innerText = q.question;\n            list.appendChild(item);\n        });\n        wrongAnswersContainer.appendChild(list);\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML += '<p>æ²’æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„ï¼</p>';\n    }\n    progressStats.appendChild(wrongAnswersContainer);\n}"
  }
}
```

## MODEL âœ¨

æˆ‘å°‡æ›´æ–° `js/script.js`ï¼šé¦–å…ˆï¼Œç²å– `explanation-container` å’Œ `explanation-text` å…ƒç´ ï¼›`startQuiz` å‡½å¼å°‡è®€å– Local Storage ä¸­çš„ `lastQuizQuestions`ï¼Œéæ¿¾æ‰å·²ç”¨é¡Œç›®ï¼Œéš¨æ©Ÿæ’åºå¾Œå–å‰ 10 é¡Œï¼Œä¸¦å°‡æ–°é¡Œç›®å­˜å› Local Storageï¼›`resetState` å‡½å¼æœƒéš±è— `explanation-container`ï¼›`selectAnswer` å’Œ `timeUp` å‡½å¼åœ¨ç­”éŒ¯æˆ–æ™‚é–“åˆ°æ™‚ï¼Œæœƒå–å¾—é¡Œç›®è§£æä¸¦é¡¯ç¤º `explanation-container`ã€‚æ¥è‘—ï¼Œæˆ‘æœƒé–‹å§‹æ’°å¯«æ›´æ–°å¾Œçš„ç¨‹å¼ç¢¼ã€‚**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "// DOM å…ƒç´ ç²å–\nconst quizContainer = document.getElementById('quiz-container');\nconst questionElement = document.getElementById('question');\nconst answerButtonsElement = document.getElementById('answer-buttons');\nconst nextButton = document.getElementById('next-btn');\nconst timerElement = document.getElementById('timer');\nconst searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');\nconst subjectFilter = document.getElementById('subject-filter');\nconst startQuizButton = document.getElementById('start-quiz-btn');\nconst filterContainer = progressStats = document.getElementById('progress-stats');\nconst explanationContainer = document.getElementById('explanation-container');\nconst explanationText = document.getElementById('explanation-text');\n\n// å…¨åŸŸè®Šæ•¸\nlet allQuestions = questions;\nlet filteredQuestions = allQuestions;\nlet shuffledQuestions, currentQuestionIndex;\nlet score = 0;\nlet timer;\nlet timeRemaining = 30;\nlet wrongAnswers = [];\n\n// åˆå§‹åŒ–\ndocument.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n    populateSubjects();\n    startQuizButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        filterQuestions();\n        startQuiz();\n    });\n    nextButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        currentQuestionIndex++;\n        setNextQuestion();\n    });\n    progressButton.addEventListener('click', toggleProgressView);\n});\n\nfunction populateSubjects() {\n    const subjects = [...new Set(allQuestions.map(q => q.subject))];\n    subjects.forEach(subject => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = subject;\n        option.innerText = subject;\n        subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n    let lastQuizQuestions = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('lastQuizQuestions')) || [];\n\n    filteredQuestions = allQuestions.filter(question => {\n        const subjectMatch = selectedSubject === 'all' || question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        // æ’é™¤ä¸Šä¸€è¼ªçš„é¡Œç›®\n        const notInLastQuiz = !lastQuizQuestions.includes(question.question);\n        return subjectMatch && searchMatch && notInLastQuiz;\n    });\n}\n\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) endResult.remove();\n    \n    questionElement.style.display = 'block';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'grid';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'block';\n\n    shuffledQuestions = filteredQuestions.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5).slice(0, 10);\n    \n    // å„²å­˜æœ¬è¼ªé¡Œç›®ï¼Œä»¥ä¾¿ä¸‹ä¸€è¼ªæ’é™¤\n    const currentQuestionText = shuffledQuestions.map(q => q.question);\n    localStorage.setItem('lastQuizQuestions', JSON.stringify(currentQuestionText));\n\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n    wrongAnswers = [];\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.innerText = 'æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„æ–°é¡Œç›®ï¼Œè«‹èª¿æ•´ç¯©é¸æ¢ä»¶æˆ–æ¸…é™¤å¿«å–å¾Œé‡è©¦ã€‚';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n}\n\nfunction setNextQuestion() {\n    resetState();\n    if (currentQuestionIndex < shuffledQuestions.length) {\n        showQuestion(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n        startTimer();\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = '';\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n        explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n        explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    }\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction setButtonStatusClass(button, correct) {\n    clearButtonStatusClass(button);\n    if (correct) {\n        button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n        timeRemaining--;\n        timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n        if (timeRemaining <= 0) {\n            clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction timeUp() {\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n    wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n    \n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, false);\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n    \n    explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction endQuiz() {\n    clearInterval(timer);\n    saveProgress();\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.style.display = 'none';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'none';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    \n    const endResult = document.createElement('div');\n    endResult.classList.add('end-result');\n    endResult.innerHTML = `\n        <h2>æ¸¬é©—çµæŸï¼</h2>\n        <p>ä½ çš„åˆ†æ•¸æ˜¯ ${score} / ${shuffledQuestions.length}</p>\n        <button id=\"restart-btn\">è¿”å›ä¸»é </button>\n    `;\n    quizContainer.appendChild(endResult);\n    \n    document.getElementById('restart-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    });\n}\n\nfunction saveProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    const subject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    if (!progress[subject]) {\n        progress[subject] = { totalScore: 0, totalQuestions: 0, wrongAnswers: [] };\n    }\n\n    progress[subject].totalScore += score;\n    progress[subject].totalQuestions += shuffledQuestions.length;\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers.push(...wrongAnswers);\n\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers = [...new Map(progress[subject].wrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    localStorage.setItem('quizProgress', JSON.stringify(progress));\n}\n\nfunction toggleProgressView() {\n    if (progressContainer.style.display === 'none') {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';\n        showProgress();\n    } else {\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    progressStats.innerHTML = '';\n\n    let totalScore = 0;\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? 'ç¸½è¦½' : subject}</h3>\n            <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n                <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${percentage}%\">${percentage}%</div>\n            </div>\n            <p>ç­”å° ${progress[subject].totalScore} / ${progress[subject].totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n        `;\n        progressStats.appendChild(subjectStat);\n    }\n\n    const overallPercentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (totalScore / totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n    const overallStat = document.createElement('div');\n    overallStat.innerHTML = `\n        <h3>ç¸½é«”é€²åº¦</h3>\n        <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n            <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${overallPercentage}%\">${overallPercentage}%</div>\n        </div>\n        <p>ç¸½ç­”å° ${totalScore} / ${totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n    `;\n    progressStats.prepend(overallStat);\n\n    const wrongAnswersContainer = document.createElement('div');\n    wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML = '<h3>éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„</h3>';\n    let allWrongAnswers = [];\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        allWrongAnswers.push(...progress[subject].wrongAnswers);\n    }\n    allWrongAnswers = [...new Map(allWrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    if (allWrongAnswers.length > 0) {\n        const list = document.createElement('ul');\n        allWrongAnswers.forEach(q => {\n            const item = document.createElement('li');\n            // Show the question and the explanation in the progress view\n            item.innerHTML = `${q.question} <br><em>è§£æï¼š${q.explanation}</em>`;\n            list.appendChild(item);\n        });\n        wrongAnswersContainer.appendChild(list);\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML += '<p>æ²’æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„ï¼</p>';\n    }\n    progressStats.appendChild(wrongAnswersContainer);\n}\n",
    "file_path": "linca-quiz-app/js/script.js"
  }
}

  "id": "read_file-1770276270218-ab77a9123df86",

  "response": {
    "output": "// DOM å…ƒç´ ç²å–\nconst quizContainer = document.getElementById('quiz-container');\nconst questionElement = document.getElementById('question');\nconst answerButtonsElement = document.getElementById('answer-buttons');\nconst nextButton = document.getElementById('next-btn');\nconst timerElement = document.getElementById('timer');\nconst searchInput = timer;\nlet timeRemaining = 30;\nlet wrongAnswers = [];\n\n// åˆå§‹åŒ–\ndocument.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n    populateSubjects();\n    startQuizButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        filterQuestions();\n        startQuiz();\n    });\n    nextButton.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        currentQuestionIndex++;\n        setNextQuestion();\n    });\n    progressButton.addEventListener('click', toggleProgressView);\n});\n\nfunction populateSubjects() {\n    const subjects = [...new Set(allQuestions.map(q => q.subject))];\n    subjects.forEach(subject => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = subject;\n        option.innerText = subject;\n        subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n    let lastQuizQuestions = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('lastQuizQuestions')) || [];\n\n    filteredQuestions = allQuestions.filter(question => {\n        const subjectMatch = selectedSubject === 'all' || question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        // æ’é™¤ä¸Šä¸€è¼ªçš„é¡Œç›®\n        const notInLastQuiz = !lastQuizQuestions.includes(question.question);\n        return subjectMatch && searchMatch && notInLastQuiz;\n    });\n}\n\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) endResult.remove();\n    \n    questionElement.style.display = 'block';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'grid';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'block';\n\n    shuffledQuestions = filteredQuestions.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5).slice(0, 10);\n    \n    // å„²å­˜æœ¬è¼ªé¡Œç›®ï¼Œä»¥ä¾¿ä¸‹ä¸€è¼ªæ’é™¤\n    const currentQuestionText = shuffledQuestions.map(q => q.question);\n    localStorage.setItem('lastQuizQuestions', JSON.stringify(currentQuestionText));\n\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n    wrongAnswers = [];\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.innerText = 'æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„æ–°é¡Œç›®ï¼Œè«‹èª¿æ•´ç¯©é¸æ¢ä»¶æˆ–æ¸…é™¤å¿«å–å¾Œé‡è©¦ã€‚';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n}\n\nfunction setNextQuestion() {\n    resetState();\n    if (currentQuestionIndex < shuffledQuestions.length) {\n        showQuestion(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n        startTimer();\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = '';\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n        explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n        explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    }\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction setButtonStatusClass(button, correct) {\n    clearButtonStatusClass(button);\n    if (correct) {\n        button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n        timeRemaining--;\n        timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n        if (timeRemaining <= 0) {\n            clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction timeUp() {\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n    wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n    \n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, false);\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n    \n    explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction endQuiz() {\n    clearInterval(timer);\n    saveProgress();\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.style.display = 'none';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'none';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    \n    const endResult = document.createElement('div');\n    endResult.classList.add('end-result');\n    endResult.innerHTML = `\n        <h2>æ¸¬é©—çµæŸï¼</h2>\n        <p>ä½ çš„åˆ†æ•¸æ˜¯ ${score} / ${shuffledQuestions.length}</p>\n        <button id=\"restart-btn\">è¿”å›ä¸»é </button>\n    `;\n    quizContainer.appendChild(endResult);\n    \n    document.getElementById('restart-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    });\n}\n\nfunction saveProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    const subject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    if (!progress[subject]) {\n        progress[subject] = { totalScore: 0, totalQuestions: 0, wrongAnswers: [] };\n    }\n\n    progress[subject].totalScore += score;\n    progress[subject].totalQuestions += shuffledQuestions.length;\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers.push(...wrongAnswers);\n\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers = [...new Map(progress[subject].wrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    localStorage.setItem('quizProgress', JSON.stringify(progress));\n}\n\nfunction toggleProgressView() {\n    if (progressContainer.style.display === 'none') {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';\n        showProgress();\n    } else {\n        progressContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    progressStats.innerHTML = '';\n\n    let totalScore = 0;\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? (totalScore / totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n    const overallStat = document.createElement('div');\n    overallStat.innerHTML = `\n        <h3>ç¸½é«”é€²åº¦</h3>\n        <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n            <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${overallPercentage}%\">${overallPercentage}%</div>\n        </div>\n        <p>ç¸½ç­”å° ${totalScore} / ${totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n    `;\n    progressStats.prepend(overallStat);\n\n    const wrongAnswersContainer = document.createElement('div');\n    wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML = '<h3>éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„</h3>';\n    let allWrongAnswers = [];\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        allWrongAnswers.push(...progress[subject].wrongAnswers);\n    }\n    allWrongAnswers = [...new Map(allWrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    if (allWrongAnswers.length > 0) {\n        const list = document.createElement('ul');\n        allWrongAnswers.forEach(q => {\n            const item = document.createElement('li');\n            // Show the question and the explanation in the progress view\n            item.innerHTML = `${q.question} <br><em>è§£æï¼š${q.explanation}</em>`;\n            list.appendChild(item);\n        });\n        wrongAnswersContainer.appendChild(list);\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML += '<p>æ²’æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„ï¼</p>';\n    }\n    progressStats.appendChild(wrongAnswersContainer);\n}\n"

languageToolsContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n\n    if (isHidden) {\n        viewContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        // If closing subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n    let question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        const notInLastQuiz = quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) endResult.remove();\n    \n    questionElement.style.display =    const currentQuestionText = shuffledQuestions.map(q => q.question);\n    localStorage.setItem('lastQuizQuestions', JSON.stringify(currentQuestionText));\n\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n    wrongAnswers = [];\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.innerText = 'æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„æ–°é¡Œç›®ï¼Œè«‹èª¿æ•´ç¯©é¸æ¢ä»¶æˆ–æ¸…é™¤å¿«å–å¾Œé‡è©¦ã€‚';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n}\n\nfunction setNextQuestion() {\n    resetState();\n    if (currentQuestionIndex < shuffledQuestions.length) {\n        showQuestion(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n        startTimer();\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = '';\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n        explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n        explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    }\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction setButtonStatusClass(button, correct) {\n    clearButtonStatusClass(button);\n    if (correct) {\n        button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n        timeRemaining--;\n        timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n        if (timeRemaining <= 0) {\n            clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction timeUp() {\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n    wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n    \n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, false);\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n    \n    explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction endQuiz() {\n    clearInterval(timer);\n    saveProgress();\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.style.display = 'none';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'none';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    \n    const endResult = document.createElement('div');\n id=\"restart-btn\">è¿”å›ä¸»é </button>\n    `;\n    quizContainer.appendChild(endResult);\n    \n    document.getElementById('restart-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n || {};\n    const subject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    if (!progress[subject]) {\n        progress[subject] = { totalScore: 0, totalQuestions: 0, wrongAnswers: [] };\n    }\n\n    progress[subject].totalScore += score;\n    progress[subject].totalQuestions += shuffledQuestions.length;\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers.push(...wrongAnswers);\n\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers = [...new Map(progress[subject].wrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    localStorage.setItem('quizProgress', JSON.stringify(progress));\n}\n\nfunction showProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    progressStats.innerHTML = '';\n\n    let totalScore = 0;\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? 'ç¸½è¦½' : subject}</h3>\n            <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n                <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${percentage}%\">${percentage}%</div>\n            </div>\n            <p>ç­”å° ${progress[subject].totalScore} / ${progress[subject].totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n        `;\n        progressStats.appendChild(subjectStat);\n    }\n\n    const overallPercentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (totalScore / totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n    const overallStat = document.createElement('div');\n    overallStat.innerHTML = `\n        <h3>ç¸½é«”é€²åº¦</h3>\n        <div const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button =>         clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction timeUp() {\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n || {};\n    const subject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    if (!progress[subject]) {\n        progress[subject] = { totalScore: 0, totalQuestions: 0, wrongAnswers: [] };\n    }\n\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? 'ç¸½è¦½' : subject}</h3>\n            <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n                <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${percentage}%\">${percentage}%</div>\n            </div>\n            <p>ç­”å° ${progress[subject].totalScore} / ${progress[subject].totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n        `;\n        progressStats.appendChild(subjectStat);\n    }\n\n    const overallPercentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (totalScore / totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n    const overallStat = document.createElement('div');\n    overallStat.innerHTML = `\n        <h3>ç¸½é«”é€²åº¦</h3>\n        <div ${totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n    `;\n    progressStats.prepend(overallStat);\n\n    const wrongAnswersContainer = document.createElement('div');\n    wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML = wrongAnswersContainer.appendChild(list);\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML += '<p>æ²’æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„ï¼</p>';\n    }\n    progressStats.appendChild(wrongAnswersContainer);\n}\n\n// Language Tools Functions\nfunction showDailyQuote() {\n    const today = new Date().toDateString();\n    let lastQuoteDate = localStorage.getItem('lastQuoteDate');\n    let quoteIndex = localStorage.getItem('quoteIndex');\n\n    if (lastQuoteDate !== today || !quoteIndex) {\n        quoteIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * quotes.length);\n        localStorage.setItem('lastQuoteDate', today);\n        localStorage.setItem('quoteIndex', quoteIndex);\n    }\n\n    const quote = quotes[quoteIndex];\n    dailyQuoteText.innerText = quote.quote;\n    dailyQuoteAuthor.innerText = `- ${quote.author}`;\n}\n\nfunction showWordCard() {\n    const word = words[currentWordIndex];\n    wordText.innerText = word.word;\n    wordPronunciation.innerText = word.pronunciation;\n    wordMeaning.innerText = word.meaning;\n    wordExample.innerText = `e.g. ${word.example}`;\n    wordCardContainer.classList.remove('flip');\n}"
  }
}
```

languageToolsContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    scienceToolsContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n\n    if (isHidden) {\n        viewContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        // If closing the current view, show the main filter/start view\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    }\n}\n\n\nfunction populateSubjects() {\n    const subjects = [...new Set(allQuestions.map(q => q.subject))];\n    subjects.forEach(subject => {\n        const option = document.createElement('option');\n        option.value = subject;\n        option.innerText = subject;\n        subjectFilter.appendChild(option);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction filterQuestions() {\n    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();\n    const selectedSubject = subjectFilter.value;\n    let lastQuizQuestions = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('lastQuizQuestions')) || [];\n\n    filteredQuestions = allQuestions.filter(question => {\n        const subjectMatch = selectedSubject === 'all' || question.subject === selectedSubject;\n        const searchMatch = question.question.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);\n        const notInLastQuiz = !lastQuizQuestions.includes(question.question);\n        return subjectMatch && searchMatch && notInLastQuiz;\n    });\n}\n\nfunction startQuiz() {\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    quizContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    \n    const endResult = quizContainer.querySelector('.end-result');\n    if (endResult) endResult.remove();\n    \n    questionElement.style.display = 'block';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'grid';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'block';\n\n    shuffledQuestions = filteredQuestions.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5).slice(0, 10);\n    \n    const currentQuestionText = shuffledQuestions.map(q => q.question);\n    localStorage.setItem('lastQuizQuestions', JSON.stringify(currentQuestionText));\n\n    currentQuestionIndex = 0;\n    score = 0;\n    wrongAnswers = [];\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > 0) {\n        setNextQuestion();\n    } else {\n        noQuestionsFound();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction noQuestionsFound() {\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.innerText = 'æ‰¾ä¸åˆ°ç¬¦åˆæ¢ä»¶çš„æ–°é¡Œç›®ï¼Œè«‹èª¿æ•´ç¯©é¸æ¢ä»¶æˆ–æ¸…é™¤å¿«å–å¾Œé‡è©¦ã€‚';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n}\n\nfunction setNextQuestion() {\n    resetState();\n    if (currentQuestionIndex < shuffledQuestions.length) {\n        showQuestion(shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex]);\n        startTimer();\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n}\n\nfunction showQuestion(question) {\n    questionElement.innerText = question.question;\n    answerButtonsElement.innerHTML = '';\n    question.answers.forEach(answer => {\n        const button = document.createElement('button');\n        button.innerText = answer.text;\n        button.classList.add('btn');\n        if (answer.correct) {\n            button.dataset.correct = answer.correct;\n        }\n        button.addEventListener('click', selectAnswer);\n        answerButtonsElement.appendChild(button);\n    });\n}\n\nfunction resetState() {\n    nextButton.style.display = 'none';\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'none';\n    while (answerButtonsElement.firstChild) {\n        answerButtonsElement.removeChild(answerButtonsElement.firstChild);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction selectAnswer(e) {\n    const selectedButton = e.target;\n    const correct = selectedButton.dataset.correct === \"true\";\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n\n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, button.dataset.correct === \"true\");\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n\n    if (correct) {\n        score++;\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n        explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n        explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n    }\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction setButtonStatusClass(button, correct) {\n    clearButtonStatusClass(button);\n    if (correct) {\n        button.classList.add('correct');\n    } else {\n        button.classList.add('wrong');\n    }\n}\n\nfunction clearButtonStatusClass(button) {\n    button.classList.remove('correct');\n    button.classList.remove('wrong');\n}\n\nfunction startTimer() {\n    timeRemaining = 30;\n    timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n    timer = setInterval(() => {\n        timeRemaining--;\n        timerElement.innerText = `å‰©é¤˜æ™‚é–“: ${timeRemaining}`;\n        if (timeRemaining <= 0) {\n            clearInterval(timer);\n            timeUp();\n        }\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction timeUp() {\n    const currentQuestion = shuffledQuestions[currentQuestionIndex];\n    wrongAnswers.push(currentQuestion);\n    \n    Array.from(answerButtonsElement.children).forEach(button => {\n        setButtonStatusClass(button, false);\n        button.disabled = true;\n    });\n    \n    explanationText.innerText = currentQuestion.explanation;\n    explanationContainer.style.display = 'block';\n\n    if (shuffledQuestions.length > currentQuestionIndex + 1) {\n        nextButton.style.display = 'block';\n    } else {\n        endQuiz();\n    }\n    clearInterval(timer);\n}\n\nfunction endQuiz() {\n    clearInterval(timer);\n    saveProgress();\n    resetState();\n    questionElement.style.display = 'none';\n    answerButtonsElement.style.display = 'none';\n    timerElement.style.display = 'none';\n    \n    const endResult = document.createElement('div');\n    endResult.classList.add('end-result');\n    endResult.innerHTML = `\n        <h2>æ¸¬é©—çµæŸï¼</h2>\n        <p>ä½ çš„åˆ†æ•¸æ˜¯ ${score} / ${shuffledQuestions.length}</p>\n        <button id=\"restart-btn\">è¿”å›ä¸»é </button>\n    `;\n    quizContainer.appendChild(endResult);\n    \n    document.getElementById('restart-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n        quizContainer.style.display = 'none';\n        filterContainer.style.display = 'flex';\n    });\n}\n\nfunction saveProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    const subject = subjectFilter.value;\n\n    if (!progress[subject]) {\n        progress[subject] = { totalScore: 0, totalQuestions: 0, wrongAnswers: [] };\n    }\n\n    progress[subject].totalScore += score;\n    progress[subject].totalQuestions += shuffledQuestions.length;\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers.push(...wrongAnswers);\n\n    progress[subject].wrongAnswers = [...new Map(progress[subject].wrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    localStorage.setItem('quizProgress', JSON.stringify(progress));\n}\n\nfunction showProgress() {\n    const progress = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('quizProgress')) || {};\n    progressStats.innerHTML = '';\n\n    let totalScore = 0;\n    let totalQuestions = 0;\n\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        totalScore += progress[subject].totalScore;\n        totalQuestions += progress[subject].totalQuestions;\n\n        const percentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (progress[subject].totalScore / progress[subject].totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n        const subjectStat = document.createElement('div');\n        subjectStat.innerHTML = `\n            <h3>${subject === 'all' ? 'ç¸½è¦½' : subject}</h3>\n            <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n                <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${percentage}%\">${percentage}%</div>\n            </div>\n            <p>ç­”å° ${progress[subject].totalScore} / ${progress[subject].totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n        `;\n        progressStats.appendChild(subjectStat);\n    }\n\n    const overallPercentage = totalQuestions > 0 ? (totalScore / totalQuestions * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;\n    const overallStat = document.createElement('div');\n    overallStat.innerHTML = `\n        <h3>ç¸½é«”é€²åº¦</h3>\n        <div class=\"progress-bar\">\n            <div class=\"progress-bar-fill\" style=\"width: ${overallPercentage}%\">${overallPercentage}%</div>\n        </div>\n        <p>ç¸½ç­”å° ${totalScore} / ${totalQuestions} é¡Œ</p>\n    `;\n    progressStats.prepend(overallStat);\n\n    const wrongAnswersContainer = document.createElement('div');\n    wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML = '<h3>éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„</h3>';\n    let allWrongAnswers = [];\n    for (const subject in progress) {\n        allWrongAnswers.push(...progress[subject].wrongAnswers);\n    }\n    allWrongAnswers = [...new Map(allWrongAnswers.map(item => [item['question'], item])).values()];\n\n    if (allWrongAnswers.length > 0) {\n        const list = document.createElement('ul');\n        allWrongAnswers.forEach(q => {\n            const item = document.createElement('li');\n            item.innerHTML = `${q.question} <br><em>è§£æï¼š${q.explanation}</em>`;\n            list.appendChild(item);\n        });\n        wrongAnswersContainer.appendChild(list);\n    } else {\n        wrongAnswersContainer.innerHTML += '<p>æ²’æœ‰éŒ¯é¡Œç´€éŒ„ï¼</p>';\n    }\n    progressStats.appendChild(wrongAnswersContainer);\n}\n\n// Language Tools Functions\nfunction showDailyQuote() {\n    const today = new Date().toDateString();\n    let lastQuoteDate = localStorage.getItem('lastQuoteDate');\n    let quoteIndex = localStorage.getItem('quoteIndex');\n\n    if (lastQuoteDate !== today || !quoteIndex) {\n        quoteIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * quotes.length);\n        localStorage.setItem('lastQuoteDate', today);\n        localStorage.setItem('quoteIndex', quoteIndex);\n    }\n\n    const quote = quotes[quoteIndex];\n    dailyQuoteText.innerText = quote.quote;\n    dailyQuoteAuthor.innerText = `- createPeriodicTable() {\n    elements.forEach(element => {\n        const elementDiv = document.createElement('div');\n        elementDiv.classList.add('element');\n (${element.symbol})</h4>\n        <p><strong>Atomic Number:</strong> ${element.number}</p>\n        <p><strong>Atomic Mass:</strong> ${element.mass}</p>\n        <p><strong>Category:</strong> ${element.category}</p>\n    `;\n    elementDetails.style.display = 'block';\n}\n",

  }
